function c_set_background_animation0
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "bg_ani_" & (($frame0 / 32) + 1))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ($frame0 mod 32) - ((($frame0 mod 32) - (30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($frame0 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))) .and. sh_right((30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($frame0 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))) - ($frame0 mod 32), 31)))
end function
function keyswitches_color_keys
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function c_subarticulation_group_count0
  $group_count01 := 0
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] = 2)
    $group_count01 := 6 * ((%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] * 3) + %subarticulations_trans_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]])
  else
    $group_count01 := (6 * %subarticulations_interval_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]]) * ((%subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]]) * (1 + %subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]]))
  end if
end function
function c_update_keyswitch_selection0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_control_par(%swi_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_control_par_str(%swi_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_key_pressed(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $idx00002 := 0
    while($idx00002 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
      if($idx00002 # $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx00002], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx00002], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      end if
      inc($idx00002)
    end while
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
    else
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
      inc($i)
    end while
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 3) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
        else
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
        end if
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real(((%modulation_positions[0] * (1 + (sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31) .or. sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)))) - sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
    @txt_keyswitch_name := !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
      inc($i)
    end while
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 3) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
        else
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
        end if
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real(((%modulation_positions[0] * (1 + (sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31) .or. sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)))) - sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
  end if
end function

function c_is_in_note_selection0
  $result01 := 0
  select($note_selection0)
    case 0
      $result01 := 1
    case 1
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx9) - 1, 31)
    case 2
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx9) - 1, 31) + - sh_right(abs($idx9 - 1) - 1, 31)
    case 3
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx9) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - (($num_pressed_notes0 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))
    case 4
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx9) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ((($num_pressed_notes0 - 2) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))
    case 5
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31)
    case 6
      $result01 := (((- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - (($num_pressed_notes0 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - $num_pressed_notes0) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - ($num_pressed_notes0 + 1), 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - (((($num_pressed_notes0 + 1) - 2) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - ($num_pressed_notes0 + 1), 31))
    case 7
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - (($num_pressed_notes0 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))
    case 8
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ((($num_pressed_notes0 - 2) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))
    case 9
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 - 1)) - 1, 31)
    case 10
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 - 1)) - 1, 31) + - sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 - 2)) - 1, 31)
    case 11
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 - 1)) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - (($num_pressed_notes0 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))
    case 12
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 - 1)) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ($num_pressed_notes0 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx9 - ((($num_pressed_notes0 - 2) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes0, 31))
    case -2147483648 to 134217727
      $result01 := 0
  end select
  $is_in_note_selection_boolean := 1 + sh_right(abs($result01) - 1, 31)
end function

  end if

function c_delay_buffer_add0
  $idx40 := search(%delay_buffer, -1)
  if($idx40 # -1)
    %delay_buffer[$idx40] := $articulation_id0
    %delay_buffer_instrument[$idx40] := $instrument0
    %delay_buffer_keyswitch[$idx40] := $keyswitch1
    %delay_buffer_subarticulation[$idx40] := $subarticulation0
    %delay_buffer_note[$idx40] := $note1
    %delay_buffer_velo[$idx40] := $velo0
    %delay_buffer_interval[$idx40] := $interval0
    %delay_buffer_countdown[$idx40] := $countdown0
    %delay_buffer_prev_note[$idx40] := $previous_note0
    $any_delay_event_queued := 1
  else
    message("WARNING: Delay Buffer Full")
  end if
end function

function c_articulations_note_off0
  $i50 := 0
  $ks10 := 0
  while($ks10 <= 7) 
    $instrument_slot0 := $instrument_slot1
    $keyswitch0 := $ks10
    $note0 := $note2
    $result22 := $result200
    call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
    $instrument_slot1 := $instrument_slot0
    $ks10 := $keyswitch0
    $note2 := $note0
    $i50 := 0
    while($i50 <= 3) 
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument_slot1 * 32) + (($ks10 * 4) + $i50)] # -1)
        $instrument_slot0 := $instrument_slot1
        $keyswitch0 := $ks10
        $note0 := $note2
        $result22 := $result210
        call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
        $articulation_id0 := 0
        $instrument0 := $instrument_slot1
        $keyswitch1 := $ks10
        $subarticulation0 := $i50
        $note1 := $note2
        $velo0 := -1
        $interval0 := 0
        $time0 := $ENGINE_UPTIME
        $countdown0 := $lookahead - %subarticulations_start_offset[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument_slot1 * 32) + (($ks10 * 4) + $i50)]]]
        $previous_note0 := -1
        $idx40 := $result210
        call c_delay_buffer_add0
        $result200 := 0
        $instrument_slot1 := $instrument0
        $ks10 := $keyswitch1
        $i50 := $subarticulation0
        $note2 := $note1
      end if
      inc($i50)
    end while
    if((($instrument_slot1 # -1) and ($ks10 # -1)) and ($note2 # -1))
      if(%_event_list[($instrument_slot1 * 1024) + (($ks10 * 128) + $note2)] >= 0)
        %_event_list[($instrument_slot1 * 1024) + (($ks10 * 128) + $note2)] := -1
      end if
    end if
    inc($ks10)
  end while
end function
function c_update_selected_notes0
  $ks20 := 0
  $pressed_key_idx := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 127) 
    if(%pressed_keys[$i] > ($ENGINE_UPTIME - $input_acceptance_time))
      $inst := 0
      while($inst <= 0) 
        $idx9 := $pressed_key_idx
        $num_pressed_notes0 := $num_pressed_keys
        $note_selection0 := %note_selections[$inst]
        $result01 := $result000
        call c_is_in_note_selection0
        $pressed_key_idx := $idx9
        $num_pressed_keys := $num_pressed_notes0
        %note_selections[$inst] := $note_selection0
        if($is_in_note_selection_boolean = 1)
          message("notens " & $i)
          $i400 := 0
          $articulation_event_id001 := 0
          $set_articulation_event_id001 := 0
          $result000 := 0
          while($result000 <= 7) 
            if(%_keyswitch_states[($inst * 8) + $result000] = 1)
              $next_free_idx0001 := -1
              $idx3001 := 0
              $i3001 := 0
              $is_free0001 := 0
              while(($next_free_idx0001 = -1) and ($idx3001 < 32)) 
                $is_free0001 := 1
                $i3001 := 0
                while($i3001 <= 3) 
                  if(%_articulation_event_list[($idx3001 * 4) + $i3001] # -1)
                    $is_free0001 := 0
                  end if
                  inc($i3001)
                end while
                $_ret110001 := 0
                $result10001 := 0
                if(search(%_event_list, $idx3001) # -1)
                  $result10001 := 1
                end if
                $_ret110001 := $result10001
                if(($is_free0001 = 1) and ($_ret110001 = 0))
                  $next_free_idx0001 := $idx3001
                end if
                $idx3001 := $idx3001 + 1
              end while
              if($next_free_idx0001 = -1)
                message("Articulation Event Buffer Full")
              end if
              $articulation_event_id001 := $next_free_idx0001
              $i400 := 0
              while($i400 <= 3) 
                if(((%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)] # -1) and ($i >= %subarticulations_range_lower[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]])) and ($i <= %subarticulations_range_upper[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]]))
                  if((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]] = 1) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]] = 0))
                    $next_free_idx0001 := 0
                    $instrument_slot0 := $inst
                    $keyswitch0 := $result000
                    $note0 := $i
                    $result22 := $result10001
                    call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
                  else
                    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]] = 3)
                      if(%_active_notes[($inst * 8) + $result000] = 0)
                        %_active_notes[($inst * 8) + $result000] := %_active_notes[($inst * 8) + $result000] + 1
                        $articulation_id0 := $articulation_event_id001
                        $instrument0 := $inst
                        $keyswitch1 := $result000
                        $subarticulation0 := $i400
                        $note1 := $i
                        $velo0 := %key_velocity[$i]
                        $interval0 := 0
                        $time0 := $ENGINE_UPTIME
                        $countdown0 := (($lookahead - %subarticulations_start_offset[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]]) + (%pressed_keys[$i] - $ENGINE_UPTIME)) + random(- %_loaded_subarticulations_humanization[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)] / 2, %_loaded_subarticulations_humanization[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)] / 2)
                        $previous_note0 := -1
                        $idx40 := $next_free_idx0001
                        call c_delay_buffer_add0
                        $next_free_idx0001 := 0
                        $articulation_event_id1 := $articulation_event_id001
                        $subarticulation1 := $i400
                        $result34 := $result10001
                        call c_articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id0
                        $set_articulation_event_id001 := 1
                      end if
                    else
                      if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]] = 2)
                        $next_free_idx0001 := 0
                        $instrument_slot0 := $inst
                        $keyswitch0 := $result000
                        $note0 := $i
                        $result22 := $result10001
                        call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
                        message($i & " note not cleared")
                      else
                        if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($inst * 32) + (($result000 * 4) + $i400)]]] = 4)
                          $next_free_idx0001 := 0
                          $instrument_slot0 := $inst
                          $keyswitch0 := $result000
                          $note0 := $i
                          $result22 := $result10001
                          call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
                        end if
                      end if
                    end if
                  end if
                end if
                inc($i400)
              end while
              if($set_articulation_event_id001 = 1)
                %_event_list[($inst * 1024) + (($result000 * 128) + $i)] := $articulation_event_id001
                %articulation_event_instrument[$articulation_event_id001] := $inst
                %articulation_event_keyswitch[$articulation_event_id001] := $result000
                %articulation_event_note[$articulation_event_id001] := $i
                message("set event id " & $articulation_event_id001 & " at " & $inst & ", " & $result000 & ", " & $i)
              end if
            end if
            inc($result000)
          end while
        else
          $ks20 := 0
          while($ks20 < 8) 
            $result000 := 0
            $instrument_slot0 := $inst
            $keyswitch0 := $ks20
            $note0 := $i
            $result22 := $i400
            call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
            $inst := $instrument_slot0
            $ks20 := $keyswitch0
            $i := $note0
            $instrument_slot1 := $inst
            $note2 := $i
            $ks10 := $i400
            $i50 := $articulation_event_id001
            $result200 := $next_free_idx0001
            $result210 := $is_free0001
            call c_articulations_note_off0
            $inst := $instrument_slot1
            $i := $note2
            $ks20 := 8
            inc($ks20)
          end while
        end if
        inc($inst)
      end while
    else
      if(%pressed_keys[$i] > 0)
        $inst := 0
        while($inst <= 0) 
          $idx9 := $pressed_key_idx
          $num_pressed_notes0 := $num_pressed_keys
          $note_selection0 := %note_selections[$inst]
          $result01 := $result000
          call c_is_in_note_selection0
          $pressed_key_idx := $idx9
          $num_pressed_keys := $num_pressed_notes0
          %note_selections[$inst] := $note_selection0
          if($is_in_note_selection_boolean = 0)
            $instrument_slot1 := $inst
            $note2 := $i
            $ks10 := $result000
            $i50 := $is_free0001
            $result200 := $set_articulation_event_id001
            $result210 := $articulation_event_id001
            call c_articulations_note_off0
            $inst := $instrument_slot1
            $i := $note2
          end if
          inc($inst)
        end while
      end if
    end if
    if(%pressed_keys[$i] > 0)
      inc($pressed_key_idx)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function

  end if
  %subarticulation_event_modulation[$subarticulation_event_id3] := $modulation0
end function
function c_articulations_compute_level0
  ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := 0.
  $fade_in_start02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch2 * 4) + $subarticulation3)]
  $fade_in_range02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch2 * 4) + $subarticulation3)]
  $fade_out_end02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch2 * 4) + $subarticulation3)]
  $fade_out_range02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch2 * 4) + $subarticulation3)]
  if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note4 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_in_start02, $fade_out_end02))
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := 1.
    if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note4 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_in_start02, $fade_in_start02 + $fade_in_range02) and ($fade_in_range02 > 0))
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := real(%modulation_positions[$note4 * $use_polyphonic_modulation] - $fade_in_start02) / real($fade_in_range02)
    else
      if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note4 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_out_end02 - $fade_out_range02, $fade_out_end02) and ($fade_out_range02 > 0))
        ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := real($fade_out_end02 - %modulation_positions[$note4 * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / real($fade_out_range02)
      end if
    end if
  end if

end function

function update_authoring_labels
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_sustain_release & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_start), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_trans_start & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 750.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (round((real($sli_trans_volume) / 1000.) * pow(10., int_to_real(2))) / pow(10., int_to_real(2))) & " dB")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeOut), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeOut) / 1000000.) * 1000.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_wait) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
end function
function c_update_authoring_transition0
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_follow), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = 1)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($vlue_authoring_start_note), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $start_note1)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($vlue_authoring_end_note), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $end_note1)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $dynamic_layer0)
    if(abs($start_note1 - $end_note1) <= 12)
      $authoring_interval_valid := 1
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note1 * 25) + (abs($end_note1 - $start_note1) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note1 - $start_note1), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_start), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note1 * 25) + (abs($end_note1 - $start_note1) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note1 - $start_note1), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note1 * 25) + (abs($end_note1 - $start_note1) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note1 - $start_note1), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note1 * 25) + (abs($end_note1 - $start_note1) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note1 - $start_note1), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_fadeOut), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note1 * 25) + (abs($end_note1 - $start_note1) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note1 - $start_note1), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note1 * 25) + (abs($end_note1 - $start_note1) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note1 - $start_note1), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note1 * 25) + (abs($end_note1 - $start_note1) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note1 - $start_note1), 31) * 12)))])
      call update_authoring_labels
    else
      $authoring_interval_valid := 0
    end if
    if($authoring_interval_valid = 1)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    else
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  end if
end function
function c_subarticulation_event_fade_out0

    fade_out(%subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id10], $fade_time1 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id10] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id10], $fade_time1 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id10] # -1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id10], $fade_time1 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id10] # -1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id10], $fade_time1 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    end if
    if($stop_voice0 = 1)
      $subarticulation_event_id5 := $subarticulation_event_id10
      $event_id0 := -1
      call c_subarticulation_event_set_event_id0
      $subarticulation_event_id10 := $subarticulation_event_id5
    end if
  end if
end function

  $transition_idx01 := 0
  $dyn_layer_idx00 := 0
  while($dyn_layer_idx00 <= 1) 
    $note_idx01 := 0
    while($note_idx01 <= 127) 
      $transition_idx01 := 0
      while($transition_idx01 <= 24) 
        %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($instrument1 * 204800) + (($keyswitch3 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx0 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($instrument1 * 204800) + (($keyswitch3 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx0 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($instrument1 * 204800) + (($keyswitch3 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx0 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($instrument1 * 204800) + (($keyswitch3 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx0 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($instrument1 * 204800) + (($keyswitch3 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx0 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($instrument1 * 204800) + (($keyswitch3 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx0 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]

function c_update_subarticulation_selection0
  $idx001 := 0
  while($idx001 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
    if($idx001 # $selected_subarticulation)
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx001], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx001], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    end if
    inc($idx001)
  end while
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real(((%modulation_positions[0] * (1 + (sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31) .or. sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)))) - sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
function subarticulation_browser_close
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
end function
function update_keyswitch_volume_curve
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_modwheel_assignment_control
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
end function
function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_dynamic_range_control
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real(((%modulation_positions[0] * (1 + (sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31) .or. sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)))) - sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
function c_angle_to_value0
  ~new_angle00 := ~angle2 + (~NI_MATH_PI / 2.)
  if(~new_angle00 > (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.))
    ~new_angle00 := ~new_angle00 - (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI)
  end if
  ~new_angle00 := abs(~new_angle00 - (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI))
  $ret130 := int((127. * (~new_angle00 - ~angle_min0)) / (~angle_max0 - ~angle_min0))
end function
on persistence_changed
  $frame0 := %CC[1]
  call c_set_background_animation0
  %CC[1] := $frame0
  $v00 := 0
  while($v00 <= 127) 
    set_key_color($v00, $KEY_COLOR_WHITE)
    if(($v00 >= 55) and ($v00 <= 96))
      set_key_color($v00, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
    end if
    inc($v00)
  end while
  call keyswitches_color_keys
  $i := 0
  $v00 := 0
  $subarticulation_id1 := 0
  $group_count01 := $group_count001
  call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  while($i <= ($v00 - 1)) 
    purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[0]] + $i) + 1, %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
    inc($i)
    call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  end while
  $i := 0
  $v00 := 0
  $subarticulation_id1 := 9
  $group_count01 := $group_count001
  call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  while($i <= ($v00 - 1)) 
    purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[9]] + $i) + 1, %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
    inc($i)
    call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  end while
  $i := 0
  $group_count001 := 0
  $subarticulation_id1 := 10
  $group_count01 := $v00
  call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  while($i <= ($group_count001 - 1)) 
    purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[10]] + $i) + 1, %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
    inc($i)
    call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  end while
  $i := 0
  $v00 := 0
  $subarticulation_id1 := 12
  $group_count01 := $group_count001
  call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  while($i <= ($v00 - 1)) 
    purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[12]] + $i) + 1, %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
    inc($i)
    call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  end while
  $i := 0
  $group_count001 := 0
  $subarticulation_id1 := 15
  $group_count01 := $v00
  call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  while($i <= ($group_count001 - 1)) 
    purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[15]] + $i) + 1, %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
    inc($i)
    call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  end while
  $i := 0
  $v00 := 0
  $subarticulation_id1 := 21
  $group_count01 := $group_count001
  call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  while($i <= ($v00 - 1)) 
    purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[21]] + $i) + 1, %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
    inc($i)
    $subarticulation_id1 := 21
    $group_count01 := $group_count001
    call c_subarticulation_group_count0
  end while
end on
on note
  ignore_event($EVENT_ID)
  set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 1)
  $group_count001 := 0
  $v00 := 0
  if(in_range($EVENT_NOTE, $keyswitch_octave * 12, (($keyswitch_octave * 12) + 8) - 1))
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 7) 
      $group_count001 := %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i]
      %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] := %KEY_DOWN[($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i]
      if($group_count001 # %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
        $v00 := 1
      end if
      $selected_keyswitch := $i
      inc($i)
    end while
    if($v00 = 1)
      $idx00002 := $idx000000
      call c_update_keyswitch_selection0
    end if
  end if
  if(%pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] = -1)
    %pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    %last_pressed[$EVENT_NOTE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    %key_velocity[$EVENT_NOTE] := $EVENT_VELOCITY
    inc($num_pressed_keys)
  end if
  $wait_time0 := $note_selection_time * 1000
  call c_wait_or_zero0
  if($NI_CALLBACK_ID = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
    $ks20 := $v00
    $result000 := $group_count001
    $i400 := $idx000000
    $articulation_event_id001 := $articulation_event_id000
    $set_articulation_event_id001 := $set_articulation_event_id000
    $next_free_idx0001 := $next_free_idx0000
    $idx3001 := $idx3000
    $i3001 := $i3000
    $is_free0001 := $is_free0000
    $_ret110001 := $_ret110000
    $result10001 := $result10000
    call c_update_selected_notes0
  end if
end on
on release
  if(get_event_mark($EVENT_ID, $MARK_1) = 0)
    set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 0)
    $last_release_callback := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
    ignore_event($EVENT_ID)
    %pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] := -1
    dec($num_pressed_keys)
    if($sustain_pedal = 0)
      message("added note off event to queue")
      $instrument_slot1 := 0
      $note2 := $EVENT_NOTE
      $ks10 := $idx000000
      $i50 := $group_count001
      $result200 := $articulation_event_id000
      $result210 := $set_articulation_event_id000
      call c_articulations_note_off0
      $wait_time0 := $note_selection_time * 1000
      call c_wait_or_zero0
      if($last_release_callback = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
        $ks20 := $set_articulation_event_id000
        $result000 := $articulation_event_id000
        $i400 := $v00
        $articulation_event_id001 := $group_count001
        $set_articulation_event_id001 := $idx000000
        $next_free_idx0001 := $i3000
        $idx3001 := $next_free_idx0000
        $i3001 := $idx3000
        $is_free0001 := $is_free0000
        $_ret110001 := $_ret110000
        $result10001 := $result10000
        call c_update_selected_notes0
      end if
    end if
  end if
end on
on controller
  ignore_controller
  %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := %CC[$CC_NUM]
  if($CC_NUM = 1)
    $frame1 := %CC[1]
    call c_buffer_modwheel_animation0
    %CC[1] := $frame1

on ui_control(?xy_modwheel_assignment)
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[1] := 1.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[5] := 1.
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN)
    if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) or (get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 4))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  else
    if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_UP)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    end if
  end if
  $ma_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 2) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]))
    if(?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] < ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2])
      ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]
    end if
    %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * 127.)
  else
    if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0])) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) - 20)))
      %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 127.))
    else
      if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 4) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4])) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]))
        set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) - 20)))
        %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 127.)
      else
        if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 6) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]))
          if(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] > ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6])
            ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]
          end if
          %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * 127.)
        end if
      end if
    end if
  end if
  wait(10000)
  if($ma_cb_id = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
    call update_modwheel_assignment_control
    call update_modwheel_assignment_circles
  end if
end on
on ui_control(?xy_dynamic_range)
  $dr_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_dynamic_range), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) and (?xy_dynamic_range[0] <= ?xy_dynamic_range[2]))
    %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * 127.)
  else
    if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_dynamic_range), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 2) and (?xy_dynamic_range[0] <= ?xy_dynamic_range[2]))
      %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * 127.)
    end if
  end if
  wait(10000)
  if($dr_cb_id = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
    call update_dynamic_range_control
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_humanize)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_humanize & " ms")
  %_loaded_subarticulations_humanization[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := $sli_humanize
end on
on ui_control(?xy_center_circles)
  $cc_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN)
    ?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := sqrt((~subarticulation_modulation_strength000 * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength000) + (~dy00 * ~dy00))
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength000 := ?xy_center_circles[0] - 0.5
    ~dy00 := ?xy_center_circles[1] - 0.5
    ~cos_theta00 := ~subarticulation_modulation_strength000 / sqrt((~subarticulation_modulation_strength000 * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength000) + (~dy00 * ~dy00))
    ~angle00 := acos(~cos_theta00)
    if(~dy00 < 0.)
      ~angle00 := (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI) - ~angle00
    end if
    $ret130 := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    ~angle2 := ?angle1[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    ~angle_min0 := 0.7
    ~angle_max0 := (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.) - 0.7
    ~new_angle00 := ~dy00
    call c_angle_to_value0
    ?angle1[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := ~angle2
    if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.32) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.36))
      $selected_subarticulation := 0
    else
      if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.36) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.4))
        $selected_subarticulation := 1
      else
        if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.4) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.44))
          $selected_subarticulation := 2
        else
          if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.44) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.48))
            $selected_subarticulation := 3
          end if
        end if
      end if
    end if
    if(abs(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] - %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) < 10)
      $selected_circle_end := 0
    else
      if(abs(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) < 10)
        $selected_circle_end := 1
      else
        $selected_circle_end := -1
      end if
    end if
    $idx001 := $set_articulation_event_id000
    call c_update_subarticulation_selection0
  end if
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG)
    wait(10000)
    if(($cc_cb_id = $NI_CALLBACK_ID) and ($selected_circle_end # -1))
      ~dy00 := ?xy_center_circles[0] - 0.5
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength000 := ?xy_center_circles[1] - 0.5
      ~cos_theta00 := ~dy00 / sqrt((~dy00 * ~dy00) + (~subarticulation_modulation_strength000 * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength000))
      ~angle00 := acos(~cos_theta00)
      if(~subarticulation_modulation_strength000 < 0.)
        ~angle00 := (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI) - ~angle00
      end if
      $ret130 := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
      ~angle2 := ?angle1[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
      ~angle_min0 := 0.7
      ~angle_max0 := (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.) - 0.7
      ~new_angle00 := ~angle00
      call c_angle_to_value0
      ?angle1[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := ~angle2
      if($selected_circle_end = 0)
        if(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < ((%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]))
          %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
        end if
      else
        if($selected_circle_end = 1)
          if(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] > ((%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]))
            %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
          end if
        end if
      end if
      call update_modwheel_assignment_control
      call update_modwheel_assignment_circles
    end if
  end if
end on

  call subarticulation_browser_close

on ui_control($btn_save_authoring)
  if($authoring_page_active = 1)
    $articulation_event_id000 := 0
    $v00 := 0
    $set_articulation_event_id000 := 0
    while($set_articulation_event_id000 <= 1) 
      $articulation_event_id000 := 0
      while($articulation_event_id000 <= 127) 
        $v00 := 0
        while($v00 <= 24) 
          %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)] := %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)]
          %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)] := %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)]
          %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)] := %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)]
          %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)]
          %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)]
          %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)]
          %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($set_articulation_event_id000 * 3200) + (($articulation_event_id000 * 25) + $v00)]
          inc($v00)
        end while
        inc($articulation_event_id000)
      end while
      inc($set_articulation_event_id000)
    end while
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_fade_in_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_release_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_wait_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_zone_start.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_zone_wait.nka")
  else
    message("No Legato Loaded")
  end if
  $btn_save_authoring := 0
end on
on ui_control($btn_load_authoring)
  if($authoring_page_active = 1)
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_fade_in_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_release_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_wait_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_zone_start.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & "_sus_trans_zone_volume.nka"))
    $instrument1 := 0
    $keyswitch3 := 0
    $subarticulation_idx0 := 0
    $dyn_layer_idx00 := $v00
    $note_idx01 := $articulation_event_id000
    $transition_idx01 := $set_articulation_event_id000
    call c_move_legato_buffer_to_instrument0
    $start_note1 := 60
    $end_note1 := 60
    $dynamic_layer0 := 0
    call c_update_authoring_transition0
  else
    message("No Legato Loaded")
  end if
  $btn_load_authoring := 0
end on
